3785  mesh.subdomainp->elementMaterialTypes[eN] = elementMaterialTypes_new[eN_global];
3786  elementNumbering_subdomain2global[eN] = eN_global;
3787  for (int nN=0;nN<mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element;nN++)
3788  {
3789  mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element+nN] =
3790  nodeNumbering_global2subdomain[elementNodesArray_new[eN_global*mesh.nNodes_element + nN]];
3791  }
3792  for (int ebN=0;ebN<mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_element;ebN++)
3793  mesh.subdomainp->elementBoundariesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_element+ebN] =
3794  elementBoundaryNumbering_global2subdomain[elementBoundariesArray_new[eN_global*mesh.nElementBoundaries_element + ebN]];
3795  }
3796 
3797  //set edge information, main piece necessary for setting subdomain data structures consistently is a map
3798  //from (nN0,nN1) --> edge_subdomain
3799  valarray<int> edgeNumbering_subdomain2global(mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global);
3800  mesh.subdomainp->edgeNodesArray = new int[mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global*2];
3801  for (int i=0; i < nEdges_subdomain_new[rank]; i++)
3802  {
3803  const int ig = i+edgeOffsets_new[rank];
3804  const int nN0_global = edgeNodesArray_newNodesAndEdges[ig*2+0];
3805  const int nN1_global = edgeNodesArray_newNodesAndEdges[ig*2+1];
3806  //mwf todo double check can always count on having nodes on this processor
3807  assert(nodeNumbering_global2subdomain.find(nN0_global) != nodeNumbering_global2subdomain.end());
3808  assert(nodeNumbering_global2subdomain.find(nN1_global) != nodeNumbering_global2subdomain.end());
3809  const int nN0_subdomain = nodeNumbering_global2subdomain[nN0_global];
3810  const int nN1_subdomain = nodeNumbering_global2subdomain[nN1_global];
3811  mesh.subdomainp->edgeNodesArray[2*i+0]=nN0_subdomain;
3812  mesh.subdomainp->edgeNodesArray[2*i+1]=nN1_subdomain;
3813  edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[i] = ig;
3814  }
3815  set<int>::iterator edge_p = edges_overlap.begin();
3816  for (int i=nEdges_subdomain_new[rank]; i < nEdges_subdomain_new[rank] + int(edges_overlap.size()); i++)
3817  {
3818  const int ig =*edge_p++;
3819  const int nN0_global = edgeNodesArray_newNodesAndEdges[ig*2+0];
3820  const int nN1_global = edgeNodesArray_newNodesAndEdges[ig*2+1];
3821  //mwf todo make sure always have nodes for the edge on this processor
3822  const int nN0_subdomain = nodeNumbering_global2subdomain[nN0_global];
3823  const int nN1_subdomain = nodeNumbering_global2subdomain[nN1_global];
3824  mesh.subdomainp->edgeNodesArray[2*i+0]=nN0_subdomain;
3825  mesh.subdomainp->edgeNodesArray[2*i+1]=nN1_subdomain;
3826  edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[i] = ig;
3827  }
3828  //now fill in rest of boundary information, etc
3829  mesh.subdomainp->px = mesh.px;
3830  mesh.subdomainp->py = mesh.py;
3831  mesh.subdomainp->pz = mesh.pz;
3832 
3833  if (mesh.px != 0)
3834  {
3835  //constructElementBoundaryElementsArrayWithGivenElementBoundaryNumbers_tetrahedron(*mesh.subdomainp);
3836  constructElementBoundaryElementsArrayWithGivenElementBoundaryAndEdgeNumbers_NURBS(*mesh.subdomainp);
3837  allocateGeometricInfo_NURBS(*mesh.subdomainp);
3838  computeGeometricInfo_NURBS(*mesh.subdomainp);
3839 
3840  }
3841  else if (mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element == 2)
3842  {
3843  //constructElementBoundaryElementsArrayWithGivenElementBoundaryNumbers_edge(*mesh.subdomainp);
3844  constructElementBoundaryElementsArrayWithGivenElementBoundaryAndEdgeNumbers_edge(*mesh.subdomainp);
3845  allocateGeometricInfo_edge(*mesh.subdomainp);
3846  computeGeometricInfo_edge(*mesh.subdomainp);
3847  }
3848 
3849  else if (mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element == 3)
3850  {
3851  //constructElementBoundaryElementsArrayWithGivenElementBoundaryNumbers_triangle(*mesh.subdomainp);
3852  constructElementBoundaryElementsArrayWithGivenElementBoundaryAndEdgeNumbers_triangle(*mesh.subdomainp);
3853  allocateGeometricInfo_triangle(*mesh.subdomainp);
3854  computeGeometricInfo_triangle(*mesh.subdomainp);
3855  }
3856  else if (mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element == 4 && mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_elementBoundary == 2)
3857  {
3858  //constructElementBoundaryElementsArrayWithGivenElementBoundaryNumbers_tetrahedron(*mesh.subdomainp);
3859  constructElementBoundaryElementsArrayWithGivenElementBoundaryAndEdgeNumbers_quadrilateral(*mesh.subdomainp);
3860  allocateGeometricInfo_quadrilateral(*mesh.subdomainp);
3861  computeGeometricInfo_quadrilateral(*mesh.subdomainp);
3862  }
3863  else if (mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element == 4)
3864  {
3865  //constructElementBoundaryElementsArrayWithGivenElementBoundaryNumbers_tetrahedron(*mesh.subdomainp);
3866  constructElementBoundaryElementsArrayWithGivenElementBoundaryAndEdgeNumbers_tetrahedron(*mesh.subdomainp);
3867  allocateGeometricInfo_tetrahedron(*mesh.subdomainp);
3868  computeGeometricInfo_tetrahedron(*mesh.subdomainp);
3869  }
3870  else if (mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element == 8)
3871  {
3872  constructElementBoundaryElementsArrayWithGivenElementBoundaryAndEdgeNumbers_hexahedron(*mesh.subdomainp);
3873  allocateGeometricInfo_hexahedron(*mesh.subdomainp);
3874  computeGeometricInfo_hexahedron(*mesh.subdomainp);
3875  }
3876  else
3877  {
3878  assert(false);
3879  }
3880  if (mesh.elementBoundaryMaterialTypes != NULL)
3881  {
3882  assert(mesh.elementBoundariesArray != NULL);
3883  //todo need to check that local element boundary numbering for
3884  //element boundaries stays the same
3885  for (int eN=0;eN<mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global;eN++)
3886  {
3887  int eN_global_new = elementNumbering_subdomain2global[eN];
3888  int eN_global_old = elementNumbering_global_new2old[eN_global_new];
3889  for (int ebN_element = 0; ebN_element < mesh.nElementBoundaries_element; ebN_element++)
3890  {
3891  int ebN_global_old = mesh.elementBoundariesArray[eN_global_old*mesh.nElementBoundaries_element+ebN_element];
3892  int ebN_subdomain = mesh.subdomainp->elementBoundariesArray[eN*mesh.nElementBoundaries_element+ebN_element];
3893  mesh.subdomainp->elementBoundaryMaterialTypes[ebN_subdomain] = mesh.elementBoundaryMaterialTypes[ebN_global_old];
3894  }
3895  }
3896  }
3897  //now we've got the old mesh in the old ordering and the subdomain mesh in the new ordering
3898  //the first chunk of nodes and elements are the owned elements so we need to know how many of those there are
3899  //and the offset of the first one so we can compute subdomain2global
3900  mesh.nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned = new int[size+1];
3901  mesh.elementOffsets_subdomain_owned = new int[size+1];
3902  mesh.elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned = new int[size+1];
3903  mesh.edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned = new int[size+1];
3904  for (int sdN=0;sdN<size+1;sdN++)
3905  {
3906  mesh.nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN] = nodeOffsets_new[sdN];
3907  mesh.elementOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN] = elementOffsets_new[sdN];
3908  mesh.elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN] = elementBoundaryOffsets_new[sdN];
3909  mesh.edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN] = edgeOffsets_new[sdN];
3910  }
3911  //we also need the subdomain 2 new global mappings
3912  mesh.nodeNumbering_subdomain2global = new int[mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global];
3913  for (int nN=0;nN<mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global;nN++)
3914  mesh.nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN] = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
3915  mesh.elementNumbering_subdomain2global = new int[mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global];
3916  for (int eN=0;eN<mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global;eN++)
3917  mesh.elementNumbering_subdomain2global[eN] = elementNumbering_subdomain2global[eN];
3918  mesh.elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global = new int[mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_global];
3919  for (int ebN=0;ebN<mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_global;ebN++)
3920  mesh.elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global[ebN] = elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global[ebN];
3921  mesh.edgeNumbering_subdomain2global = new int[mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global];
3922  for (int i=0; i< mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global; i++)
3923  mesh.edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[i] = edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
3924 
3925  //
3926  //go ahead and renumber global mesh
3927  //
3928  //std::cout<<"nodeArray"<<std::endl;
3929  for (int i=0;i<mesh.nNodes_global*3;i++)
3930  mesh.nodeArray[i] = nodeArray_new[i];
3931  //std::cout<<"elementNodesArray"<<std::endl;
3932  for (int i=0;i<mesh.nElements_global*mesh.nNodes_element;i++)
3933  mesh.elementNodesArray[i] = elementNodesArray_new[i];
3934  //std::cout<<"elementBoundaryNodesArray"<<std::endl;
3935  for (int i=0;i<mesh.nElementBoundaries_global*mesh.nNodes_elementBoundary;i++)
3936  mesh.elementBoundaryNodesArray[i] = elementBoundaryNodesArray_new[i];
3937  //std::cout<<"edgeNodesArray"<<std::endl;
3938  for (int i=0;i<mesh.nEdges_global*2;i++)
3939  mesh.edgeNodesArray[i] = edgeNodesArray_newNodesAndEdges[i];
3940  //std::cout<<"nodeStarArray"<<std::endl;
3941  for (int i=0;i<mesh.nodeStarOffsets[mesh.nNodes_global];i++)
3942  mesh.nodeStarArray[i] = nodeStarArray_new[i];
3943  //std::cout<<"elementNeighborsArray"<<std::endl;
3944  for (int i=0; i<mesh.nElements_global*mesh.nElementBoundaries_element; i++)
3945  mesh.elementNeighborsArray[i] = elementNeighborsArray_new[i];
3946  //std::cout<<"elementBoundariesArray"<<std::endl;
3947  for (int i=0; i<mesh.nElements_global*mesh.nElementBoundaries_element; i++)
3948  mesh.elementBoundariesArray[i] = elementBoundariesArray_new[i];
3949  //std::cout<<"elementBoundaryElementsArray"<<std::endl;
3950  for (int i=0; i<mesh.nElementBoundaries_global*2; i++)
3951  mesh.elementBoundaryElementsArray[i] = elementBoundaryElementsArray_new[i];
3952  //std::cout<<"elementBoundaryLocalElementBoundariesArray"<<std::endl;
3953  for (int i=0; i<mesh.nElementBoundaries_global*2; i++)
3954  mesh.elementBoundaryLocalElementBoundariesArray[i] = elementBoundaryLocalElementBoundariesArray_new[i];
3955  //
3956  //need material properties too
3957  //
3958  if (mesh.elementMaterialTypes != NULL)
3959  {
3960  //std::cout<<"elementMaterialTypes"<<std::endl;
3961  for (int i=0; i < mesh.nElements_global; i++)
3962  mesh.elementMaterialTypes[i] = elementMaterialTypes_new[i];
3963  }
3964  if (mesh.elementBoundaryMaterialTypes != NULL)
3965  {
3966  //std::cout<<"elementBoundaryMaterialTypes"<<std::endl;
3967  for (int i=0; i < mesh.nElementBoundaries_global; i++)
3968  mesh.elementBoundaryMaterialTypes[i] = elementBoundaryMaterialTypes_new[i];
3969  }
3970 
3971  ISRestoreIndices(elementNumberingIS_global_old2new,&elementNumbering_global_old2new);
3972 
3973  ISDestroy(&elementPartitioningIS_new);
3974  ISDestroy(&elementNumberingIS_subdomain_old2new);
3975  ISDestroy(&elementNumberingIS_global_old2new);
3976 
3977  ISRestoreIndices(nodeNumberingIS_global_new2old,&nodeNumbering_global_new2old);
3978 
3979  ISDestroy(&nodeNumberingIS_new2old);
3980  ISDestroy(&nodeNumberingIS_global_new2old);
3981 
3982  ISRestoreIndices(elementBoundaryNumberingIS_global_new2old,&elementBoundaryNumbering_global_new2old);
3983 
3984  ISDestroy(&elementBoundaryNumberingIS_new2old);
3985  ISDestroy(&elementBoundaryNumberingIS_global_new2old);
3986 
3987  ISRestoreIndices(edgeNumberingIS_global_new2old,&edgeNumbering_global_new2old);
3988 
3989  ISDestroy(&edgeNumberingIS_new2old);
3990  ISDestroy(&edgeNumberingIS_global_new2old);
3991 
3992  return 0;
3993 }
3994 
3995 int buildQuadraticSubdomain2GlobalMappings_1d(const MPI_Comm& PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD, Mesh& mesh,
3996  const int *elementOffsets_subdomain_owned,
3997  const int *nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned,
3998  const int *elementNumbering_subdomain2global,
3999  const int *nodeNumbering_subdomain2global,
4000  int& nDOF_all_processes,//total number of dofs in whole domain
4001  int& nDOF_subdomain,//total number of dofs in sub-domain
4002  int& max_dof_neighbors,//maximum number of neighbors for connectivity of dofs
4003  int *offsets_subdomain_owned, //starting point of local dofs on each processor (nProcs+1)
4004  int * subdomain_l2g, //local to global dof mapping on subdomain
4005  int* subdomain2global,//subdomain dof to global (parallel) numbering
4006  double * lagrangeNodesArray)//location of nodes corresponding to dofs
4007 {
4008  using namespace std;
4009  int ierr,size,rank;
4010 
4011  ierr = MPI_Comm_size(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,&size);
4012  ierr = MPI_Comm_rank(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,&rank);
4013 
4014 
4015  //In 1d the quadratic dofs can be associated with nodes and elements
4016  //assuming have ownership info and consistent local/global mappings for nodes, elements
4017  //build a mapping from local quadratic dofs to global quadratic dofs for petsc
4018  //assume a processor owns a dof if it owns that node or element
4019  assert(elementOffsets_subdomain_owned);
4020  assert(nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned);
4021  assert(elementNumbering_subdomain2global);
4022  assert(nodeNumbering_subdomain2global);
4023  assert(mesh.subdomainp);
4024 
4025  const int nNodes_owned = nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank+1]-nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank];
4026  const int nElements_owned = elementOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank+1]-elementOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank];
4027 
4028  //start with a logical global ordering of dofs as
4029  //[global nodes, global elements]
4030  //want to create global numbering
4031  //[nodes proc 0,elements proc 0,nodes proc 1, elements proc 1,...]
4032  valarray<int> quadraticNumbering_new2old(nNodes_owned + nElements_owned);
4033  for (int nN = 0; nN < nNodes_owned; nN++)
4034  {
4035  int dof_global = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4036  quadraticNumbering_new2old[nN] = dof_global;
4037  }
4038  for (int eN = 0; eN < nElements_owned; eN++)
4039  {
4040  int dof_global = mesh.nNodes_global + elementNumbering_subdomain2global[eN];
4041  quadraticNumbering_new2old[nNodes_owned + eN] = dof_global;
4042  }
4043 
4044  //build an index set for new numbering
4045  IS quadraticNumberingIS_new2old;
4046  ISCreateGeneral(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,nNodes_owned + nElements_owned,&quadraticNumbering_new2old[0],PETSC_COPY_VALUES,&quadraticNumberingIS_new2old);
4047  IS quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old;
4048  ISAllGather(quadraticNumberingIS_new2old,&quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old);
4049  //get old 2 new mapping for dofs
4050  const PetscInt *quadraticNumbering_global_new2old;
4051  valarray<int> quadraticNumbering_old2new_global(mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nElements_global);
4052  ISGetIndices(quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old,&quadraticNumbering_global_new2old);
4053  for (int id = 0; id < mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nElements_global; id++)
4054  quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]] = id;
4055  // //mwf debug
4056  // for (int id = 0; id < mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nElements_global; id++)
4057  // {
4058  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" build c0p2 mappings new2old["<<id<<"]= "<<quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]
4059  // <<" old2new["<<quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]<<"]= "<<quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]]
4060  // <<std::endl;
4061  // }
4062  assert(offsets_subdomain_owned);
4063  assert(subdomain2global);
4064  assert(subdomain_l2g);
4065  assert(lagrangeNodesArray);
4066  nDOF_all_processes = mesh.nNodes_global+mesh.nElements_global;
4067  nDOF_subdomain = mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global+mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global;
4068  max_dof_neighbors = 2*mesh.max_nNodeNeighbors_node;
4069 
4070  for (int sdN=0; sdN < size+1; sdN++)
4071  offsets_subdomain_owned[sdN] = nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN]+elementOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN];
4072 
4073  //loop through owned and ghost dofs build subdomain mapping by
4074  //going from old --> new
4075  int localOffset = 0;
4076  for (int nN = 0; nN < nNodes_owned; nN++)
4077  {
4078  int dof_global_old = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4079  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4080  subdomain2global[localOffset + nN] = dof_global_new;
4081  //mwf debug
4082  //std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" nN= "<<nN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+nN<<" nNodes_owned= "<<nNodes_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4083  }
4084  localOffset += nNodes_owned;
4085  for (int eN = 0; eN < nElements_owned; eN++)
4086  {
4087  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + elementNumbering_subdomain2global[eN];
4088  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4089  subdomain2global[localOffset + eN] = dof_global_new;
4090  //mwf debug
4091  //std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" eN= "<<eN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+eN<<" nElements_owned= "<<nElements_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4092  }
4093  localOffset += nElements_owned;
4094  for (int nN = nNodes_owned; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global; nN++)
4095  {
4096  int dof_global_old = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4097  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4098  subdomain2global[localOffset + nN -nNodes_owned] = dof_global_new;
4099  //mwf debug
4100  //std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" nN= "<<nN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+nN-nNodes_owned<<" nNodes_owned= "<<nNodes_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4101  }
4102  localOffset += mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global - nNodes_owned;
4103  for (int eN = nElements_owned; eN < mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global; eN++)
4104  {
4105  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + elementNumbering_subdomain2global[eN];
4106  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4107  subdomain2global[localOffset + eN-nElements_owned] = dof_global_new;
4108  //mwf debug
4109  //std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" eN= "<<eN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+eN-nElements_owned<<" nElements_owned= "<<nElements_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4110  }
4111  //setup local to global mapping on the subdomain for finite elements
4112  const int nDOF_element = 3;
4113  const int ghostNodeOffset = nNodes_owned + nElements_owned;
4114  const int ghostElementOffset = ghostNodeOffset + mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global-nNodes_owned;
4115 
4116  //for lagrange nodes
4117  int nN_global_subdomain[2];
4118  for (int eN=0; eN < mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global; eN++)
4119  {
4120  for (int nN=0; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element; nN++)
4121  {
4122  nN_global_subdomain[nN] = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + nN];
4123  if (nN_global_subdomain[nN] < nNodes_owned)
4124  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+nN] = nN_global_subdomain[nN];
4125  else
4126  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+nN] = nN_global_subdomain[nN]-nNodes_owned + ghostNodeOffset;
4127  //vertex dof
4128  for (int eI=0; eI < 3; eI++)
4129  lagrangeNodesArray[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+nN]*3+eI] = mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[3*nN_global_subdomain[nN]+eI];
4130  }
4131  if (eN < nElements_owned)
4132  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+2] = nNodes_owned + eN;
4133  else
4134  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+2] = eN - nElements_owned + ghostElementOffset;
4135  //vertex dof
4136  for (int eI=0; eI < 3; eI++)
4137  lagrangeNodesArray[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+2]*3+eI] = 0.5*(mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[3*nN_global_subdomain[0]+eI]+mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[3*nN_global_subdomain[1]+eI]);
4138  }
4139 
4140  ISRestoreIndices(quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old,&quadraticNumbering_global_new2old);
4141  ISDestroy(&quadraticNumberingIS_new2old);
4142  ISDestroy(&quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old);
4143 
4144  return 0;
4145 }
4146 
4147 int buildQuadraticSubdomain2GlobalMappings_2d(const MPI_Comm& PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD, Mesh& mesh,
4148  const int *elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned,
4149  const int *nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned,
4150  const int *elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global,
4151  const int *nodeNumbering_subdomain2global,
4152  int& nDOF_all_processes,//total number of dofs in whole domain
4153  int& nDOF_subdomain,//total number of dofs in sub-domain
4154  int& max_dof_neighbors,//maximum number of neighbors for connectivity of dofs
4155  int *offsets_subdomain_owned, //starting point of local dofs on each processor (nProcs+1)
4156  int *subdomain_l2g, //local to global dof mapping on subdomain
4157  int *subdomain2global,//subdomain dof to global (parallel) numbering
4158  double * lagrangeNodesArray)//location of nodes corresponding to dofs
4159 {
4160  using namespace std;
4161  int ierr,size,rank;
4162 
4163  ierr = MPI_Comm_size(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,&size);
4164  ierr = MPI_Comm_rank(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,&rank);
4165 
4166  //In 2d the quadratic dofs can be associated with nodes and element Boundaries
4167  //assuming have ownership info and consistent local/global mappings for nodes, elementBoundaries
4168  //build a mapping from local quadratic dofs to global quadratic dofs for petsc
4169  //assume a processor owns a dof if it owns that node or element
4170  assert(elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned);
4171  assert(nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned);
4172  assert(elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global);
4173  assert(nodeNumbering_subdomain2global);
4174  assert(mesh.subdomainp);
4175 
4176  const int nNodes_owned = nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank+1]-nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank];
4177  const int nElementBoundaries_owned = elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank+1]-elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank];
4178  const int nDOFs_owned = nNodes_owned + nElementBoundaries_owned;
4179  const int nDOFs_global= mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nElementBoundaries_global;
4180  //start with a logical global ordering of dofs as
4181  //[global nodes, global elementBoundaries]
4182  //want to create global numbering
4183  //[nodes proc 0,elementBoundaries proc 0,nodes proc 1, elementBoundaries proc 1,...]
4184  valarray<int> quadraticNumbering_new2old(nDOFs_owned);
4185  for (int nN = 0; nN < nNodes_owned; nN++)
4186  {
4187  int dof_global = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4188  quadraticNumbering_new2old[nN] = dof_global;
4189  }
4190  for (int ebN = 0; ebN < nElementBoundaries_owned; ebN++)
4191  {
4192  int dof_global = mesh.nNodes_global + elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global[ebN];
4193  quadraticNumbering_new2old[nNodes_owned + ebN] = dof_global;
4194  }
4195 
4196  //build an index set for new numbering
4197  IS quadraticNumberingIS_new2old;
4198  ISCreateGeneral(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,nDOFs_owned,&quadraticNumbering_new2old[0],PETSC_COPY_VALUES,&quadraticNumberingIS_new2old);
4199  IS quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old;
4200  ISAllGather(quadraticNumberingIS_new2old,&quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old);
4201  //get old 2 new mapping for dofs
4202  const PetscInt *quadraticNumbering_global_new2old;
4203  valarray<int> quadraticNumbering_old2new_global(nDOFs_global);
4204  ISGetIndices(quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old,&quadraticNumbering_global_new2old);
4205  for (int id = 0; id < nDOFs_global; id++)
4206  quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]] = id;
4207  //mwf debug
4208  //for (int id = 0; id < nDOFs_global; id++)
4209  // {
4210  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" build 2d c0p2 mappings new2old["<<id<<"]= "<<quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]
4211  // <<" old2new["<<quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]<<"]= "<<quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]]
4212  // <<std::endl;
4213  // }
4214  assert(offsets_subdomain_owned);
4215  assert(subdomain2global);
4216  assert(subdomain_l2g);
4217  assert(lagrangeNodesArray);
4218  for (int sdN=0; sdN < size+1; sdN++)
4219  offsets_subdomain_owned[sdN] = nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN]+elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN];
4220  nDOF_all_processes = mesh.nNodes_global+mesh.nElementBoundaries_global;
4221  nDOF_subdomain = mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global+mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_global;
4222  max_dof_neighbors = 2*mesh.max_nNodeNeighbors_node;
4223 
4224  //loop through owned and ghost dofs build subdomain mapping by
4225  //going from old --> new
4226  int localOffset = 0;
4227  for (int nN = 0; nN < nNodes_owned; nN++)
4228  {
4229  int dof_global_old = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4230  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4231  subdomain2global[localOffset + nN] = dof_global_new;
4232  //mwf debug
4233  //std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" nN= "<<nN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+nN<<" nNodes_owned= "<<nNodes_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4234  }
4235  localOffset += nNodes_owned;
4236  for (int ebN = 0; ebN < nElementBoundaries_owned; ebN++)
4237  {
4238  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global[ebN];
4239  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4240  subdomain2global[localOffset + ebN] = dof_global_new;
4241  //mwf debug
4242  //std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" ebN= "<<ebN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+ebN<<" nElementBoundaries_owned= "<<nElementBoundaries_owned
4243  // <<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4244  }
4245  localOffset += nElementBoundaries_owned;
4246  for (int nN = nNodes_owned; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global; nN++)
4247  {
4248  int dof_global_old = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4249  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4250  subdomain2global[localOffset + nN -nNodes_owned] = dof_global_new;
4251  //mwf debug
4252  //std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" nN= "<<nN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+nN-nNodes_owned<<" nNodes_owned= "<<nNodes_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4253  }
4254  localOffset += mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global - nNodes_owned;
4255  for (int ebN = nElementBoundaries_owned; ebN < mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_global; ebN++)
4256  {
4257  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global[ebN];
4258  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4259  subdomain2global[localOffset + ebN-nElementBoundaries_owned] = dof_global_new;
4260  //mwf debug
4261  //std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" ebN= "<<ebN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+ebN-nElementBoundaries_owned<<" nElementBoundaries_owned= "<<nElementBoundaries_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4262  }
4263  //setup local to global mapping on the subdomain for finite elements
4264  const int nDOF_element = 6;
4265  const int ghostNodeOffset = nNodes_owned + nElementBoundaries_owned;
4266  const int ghostElementBoundaryOffset = ghostNodeOffset + mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global-nNodes_owned;
4267 
4268  //for lagrange nodes
4269  int nN_global_subdomain[3];
4270  for (int eN=0; eN < mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global; eN++)
4271  {
4272  for (int nN=0; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element; nN++)
4273  {
4274  nN_global_subdomain[nN] = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + nN];
4275  if (nN_global_subdomain[nN] < nNodes_owned)
4276  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+nN] = nN_global_subdomain[nN];
4277  else
4278  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+nN] = nN_global_subdomain[nN]-nNodes_owned + ghostNodeOffset;
4279  //vertex dof
4280  for (int eI=0; eI < 3; eI++)
4281  lagrangeNodesArray[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+nN]*3+eI] = mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[3*nN_global_subdomain[nN]+eI];
4282  }
4283  for (int ebN=0; ebN < mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_element; ebN++)
4284  {
4285  //take into account numbering of edges according to
4286  //vertex they are across from
4287  int ebN_global = mesh.subdomainp->elementBoundariesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_element+((ebN+2)%3)];
4288  if (ebN_global < nElementBoundaries_owned)
4289  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+3+ebN] = nNodes_owned + ebN_global;
4290  else
4291  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+3+ebN] = ebN_global - nElementBoundaries_owned + ghostElementBoundaryOffset;
4292  //center of edge dof
4293  for (int eI=0; eI < 3; eI++)
4294  lagrangeNodesArray[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+3+ebN]*3+eI] = 0.5*(mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[3*nN_global_subdomain[(ebN+0)%3]+eI]+mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[3*nN_global_subdomain[(ebN+1)%3]+eI]);
4295  }
4296  }//eN
4297 
4298  ISRestoreIndices(quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old,&quadraticNumbering_global_new2old);
4299  ISDestroy(&quadraticNumberingIS_new2old);
4300  ISDestroy(&quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old);
4301 
4302  return 0;
4303 }
4304 
4305 
4306 int buildQuadraticSubdomain2GlobalMappings_3d(const MPI_Comm& PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD, Mesh& mesh,
4307  const int *edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned,
4308  const int *nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned,
4309  const int *edgeNumbering_subdomain2global,
4310  const int *nodeNumbering_subdomain2global,
4311  int& nDOF_all_processes,//total number of dofs in whole domain
4312  int& nDOF_subdomain,//total number of dofs in sub-domain
4313  int& max_dof_neighbors,//maximum number of neighbors for connectivity of dofs
4314  int *offsets_subdomain_owned, //starting point of local dofs on each processor (nProcs+1)
4315  int *subdomain_l2g, //local to global dof mapping on subdomain
4316  int *subdomain2global,//subdomain dof to global (parallel) numbering
4317  double * lagrangeNodesArray)//location of nodes corresponding to dofs
4318 {
4319  using namespace std;
4320  int ierr,size,rank;
4321 
4322  ierr = MPI_Comm_size(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,&size);
4323  ierr = MPI_Comm_rank(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,&rank);
4324 
4325  //In 2d the quadratic dofs can be associated with nodes and element Boundaries
4326  //assuming have ownership info and consistent local/global mappings for nodes, elementBoundaries
4327  //build a mapping from local quadratic dofs to global quadratic dofs for petsc
4328  //assume a processor owns a dof if it owns that node or element
4329  assert(edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned);
4330  assert(nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned);
4331  assert(edgeNumbering_subdomain2global);
4332  assert(nodeNumbering_subdomain2global);
4333  assert(mesh.subdomainp);
4334 
4335  const int nNodes_owned = nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank+1]-nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank];
4336  const int nEdges_owned = edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank+1]-edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank];
4337  const int nDOFs_owned = nNodes_owned + nEdges_owned;
4338  const int nDOFs_global= mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nEdges_global;
4339  //start with a logical global ordering of dofs as
4340  //[global nodes, global edges]
4341  //want to create global numbering
4342  //[nodes proc 0,edges proc 0,nodes proc 1, edges proc 1,...]
4343  valarray<int> quadraticNumbering_new2old(nDOFs_owned);
4344  for (int nN = 0; nN < nNodes_owned; nN++)
4345  {
4346  int dof_global = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4347  quadraticNumbering_new2old[nN] = dof_global;
4348  }
4349  for (int i = 0; i < nEdges_owned; i++)
4350  {
4351  int dof_global = mesh.nNodes_global + edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4352  quadraticNumbering_new2old[nNodes_owned + i] = dof_global;
4353  }
4354 
4355  //build an index set for new numbering
4356  IS quadraticNumberingIS_new2old;
4357  ISCreateGeneral(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,nDOFs_owned,&quadraticNumbering_new2old[0],PETSC_COPY_VALUES,&quadraticNumberingIS_new2old);
4358  IS quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old;
4359  ISAllGather(quadraticNumberingIS_new2old,&quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old);
4360  //get old 2 new mapping for dofs
4361  const PetscInt *quadraticNumbering_global_new2old;
4362  valarray<int> quadraticNumbering_old2new_global(nDOFs_global);
4363  ISGetIndices(quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old,&quadraticNumbering_global_new2old);
4364  for (int id = 0; id < nDOFs_global; id++)
4365  quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]] = id;
4366  //mwf debug
4367  // if (rank == 0)
4368  // {
4369  // for (int id = 0; id < nDOFs_global; id++)
4370  // {
4371  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" build 2d c0p2 mappings new2old["<<id<<"]= "<<quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]
4372  // <<" old2new["<<quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]<<"]= "<<quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]]
4373  // <<std::endl;
4374  // }
4375  // }
4376  assert(offsets_subdomain_owned);
4377  assert(subdomain2global);
4378  assert(subdomain_l2g);
4379  assert(lagrangeNodesArray);
4380  for (int sdN=0; sdN < size+1; sdN++)
4381  offsets_subdomain_owned[sdN] = nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN]+edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN];
4382  nDOF_all_processes = mesh.nNodes_global+mesh.nEdges_global;
4383  nDOF_subdomain = mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global+mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global;
4384  max_dof_neighbors = 2*mesh.max_nNodeNeighbors_node;
4385 
4386  //loop through owned and ghost dofs build subdomain mapping by
4387  //going from old --> new
4388  int localOffset = 0;
4389  for (int nN = 0; nN < nNodes_owned; nN++)
4390  {
4391  int dof_global_old = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4392  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4393  subdomain2global[localOffset + nN] = dof_global_new;
4394  //mwf debug
4395  // if (rank == 0)
4396  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" nN= "<<nN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+nN<<" nNodes_owned= "<<nNodes_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4397  }
4398  localOffset += nNodes_owned;
4399  for (int i = 0; i < nEdges_owned; i++)
4400  {
4401  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4402  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4403  subdomain2global[localOffset + i] = dof_global_new;
4404  //mwf debug
4405  // if (rank == 0)
4406  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" i= "<<i<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+i<<" nEdges_owned= "<<nEdges_owned
4407  // <<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4408  }
4409  localOffset += nEdges_owned;
4410  for (int nN = nNodes_owned; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global; nN++)
4411  {
4412  int dof_global_old = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4413  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4414  subdomain2global[localOffset + nN -nNodes_owned] = dof_global_new;
4415  //mwf debug
4416  // if (rank == 0)
4417  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" nN= "<<nN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+nN-nNodes_owned<<" nNodes_owned= "<<nNodes_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4418  }
4419  localOffset += mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global - nNodes_owned;
4420  for (int i = nEdges_owned; i < mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global; i++)
4421  {
4422  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4423  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4424  subdomain2global[localOffset + i-nEdges_owned] = dof_global_new;
4425  // //mwf debug
4426  // if (rank == 0)
4427  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" i= "<<i<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+i-nEdges_owned<<" nEdges_owned= "<<nEdges_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4428  }
4429  //setup local to global mapping on the subdomain for finite elements
4430  const int nDOF_element = 10;
4431  const int ghostNodeOffset = nNodes_owned + nEdges_owned;
4432  const int ghostEdgeOffset = ghostNodeOffset + mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global-nNodes_owned;
4433  //need mapping from nodes to edge to setup element based relationship
4434  map<NodeTuple<2>, int> nodesEdgeMap_subdomain;
4435  for (int i=0; i < mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global; i++)
4436  {
4437  int nodes[2];
4438  nodes[0] = mesh.subdomainp->edgeNodesArray[2*i];
4439  nodes[1] = mesh.subdomainp->edgeNodesArray[2*i+1];
4440  NodeTuple<2> et(nodes);
4441  const int nN0 = mesh.subdomainp->edgeNodesArray[2*i];
4442  const int nN1 = mesh.subdomainp->edgeNodesArray[2*i+1];
4443  nodesEdgeMap_subdomain[et] = i;
4444  }
4445  for (int eN=0; eN < mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global; eN++)
4446  {
4447  int local_offset = 0;
4448  for (int nN=0; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element; nN++)
4449  {
4450  //node_i --> unique subdomain node 0 <= i <= 3
4451  const int nN_global_subdomain = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + nN];
4452  //assign unique subdomain id based on |owned nodes|owned edges|ghost nodes|ghost edges|
4453  if (nN_global_subdomain < nNodes_owned)
4454  {
4455  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = nN_global_subdomain;
4456  }
4457  else
4458  {
4459  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = ghostNodeOffset + nN_global_subdomain - nNodes_owned;
4460  }
4461  //unique subdomain id --> unique cross processor id
4462  //subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]] = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN_global_subdomain];
4463  //mwf debug
4464  // if (rank == 0)
4465  // {
4466  // std::cout<<"build loc2glob c0p2 3d eN= "<<eN<<" node= "<<nN<<" sub_dof= "<< subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]
4467  // <<" glob_dof= "<<subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]]<<std::endl;
4468  // }
4469  for (int eI=0; eI < 3; eI++)
4470  lagrangeNodesArray[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset +nN]*3+eI] = mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nN_global_subdomain*3+eI];
4471  }
4472  local_offset += mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element;
4473  //(node_i,node_{i+1}) --> unique subdomain edge, 0 <= i < 3
4474  for (int nN = 0; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element-1; nN++)
4475  {
4476  const int nN_neig = (nN+1)%mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element;
4477  const int nN_global_subdomain = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + nN];
4478  const int nN_neig_global_subdomain= mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + nN_neig];
4479  //unique edge subdomain id and global id
4480  int edge_subdomain = -1,edge_global=-1;
4481  //see if edge is (nN,nN_neig) or vice versa
4482  int nodes[2];
4483  nodes[0] = nN_global_subdomain;
4484  nodes[1] = nN_neig_global_subdomain;
4485  NodeTuple<2> et(nodes);
4486  edge_subdomain = nodesEdgeMap_subdomain[et];
4487  edge_global = edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[edge_subdomain];
4488  assert(edge_subdomain >= 0 && edge_global >= 0);
4489 
4490  //assign unique subdomain id based on |owned nodes|owned edges|ghost nodes|ghost edges|
4491  if (edge_subdomain < nEdges_owned)
4492  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = nNodes_owned + edge_subdomain;
4493  else
4494  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = ghostEdgeOffset + edge_subdomain - nEdges_owned;
4495  //unique subdomain id --> unique cross processor id
4496  //set above could do here subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]] = mesh.nNodes_global + edge_global;
4497  //mwf debug
4498  // if (rank == 0)
4499  // {
4500  // std::cout<<"build loc2glob c0p2 3d eN= "<<eN<<" edge("<<nN<<","<<nN_neig<<") sub_dof= "<< subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]
4501  // <<" glob_dof= "<<subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]]<<std::endl;
4502  // }
4503  for (int eI=0; eI < 3; eI++)
4504  lagrangeNodesArray[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+local_offset+nN]*3+eI] = 0.5*(mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nN_global_subdomain*3+eI]+
4505  mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nN_neig_global_subdomain*3+eI]);
4506  }
4507  local_offset += mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element-1;
4508  //(node_i,node_{i+2}) --> unique subdomain edge, 0 <= i < 2
4509  for (int nN = 0; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element-2; nN++)
4510  {
4511  const int nN_neig = (nN+2)%mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element;
4512  const int nN_global_subdomain = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + nN];
4513  const int nN_neig_global_subdomain= mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + nN_neig];
4514  //unique edge subdomain id and global id
4515  int edge_subdomain = -1, edge_global = -1;
4516  //see if edge is (nN,nN_neig) or vice versa
4517  int nodes[2];
4518  nodes[0] = nN_global_subdomain;
4519  nodes[1] = nN_neig_global_subdomain;
4520  NodeTuple<2> et(nodes);
4521  edge_subdomain = nodesEdgeMap_subdomain[et];
4522  edge_global = edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[edge_subdomain];
4523  assert(edge_subdomain >= 0 && edge_global >= 0);
4524  //assign unique subdomain id based on |owned nodes|owned edges|ghost nodes|ghost edges|
4525  if (edge_subdomain < nEdges_owned)
4526  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = nNodes_owned + edge_subdomain;
4527  else
4528  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = ghostEdgeOffset + edge_subdomain - nEdges_owned;
4529  //unique subdomain id --> unique cross processor id
4530  //subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]] = mesh.nNodes_global + edge_global;
4531  //mwf debug
4532  // if (rank == 0)
4533  // {
4534  // std::cout<<"build loc2glob c0p2 3d eN= "<<eN<<" edge("<<nN<<","<<nN_neig<<") sub_dof= "<< subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]
4535  // <<" glob_dof= "<<subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]]<<std::endl;
4536  // }
4537  for (int eI=0; eI < 3; eI++)
4538  lagrangeNodesArray[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+local_offset+nN]*3+eI] = 0.5*(mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nN_global_subdomain*3+eI]+
4539  mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nN_neig_global_subdomain*3+eI]);
4540  }
4541  local_offset += mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element-2;
4542  //(node_i,node_{i+3}) --> unique subdomain edge, 0 = i
4543  for (int nN = 0; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element-3; nN++)
4544  {
4545  const int nN_neig = (nN+3)%mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element;
4546  const int nN_global_subdomain = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + nN];
4547  const int nN_neig_global_subdomain= mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + nN_neig];
4548  //unique edge subdomain id and global id
4549  int edge_subdomain = -1, edge_global = -1;
4550  //see if edge is (nN,nN_neig) or vice versa
4551  int nodes[2];
4552  nodes[0] = nN_global_subdomain;
4553  nodes[1] = nN_neig_global_subdomain;
4554  NodeTuple<2> et(nodes);
4555  edge_subdomain = nodesEdgeMap_subdomain[et];
4556  edge_global = edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[edge_subdomain];
4557  assert(edge_subdomain >= 0 && edge_global >= 0);
4558  //assign unique subdomain id based on |owned nodes|owned edges|ghost nodes|ghost edges|
4559  if (edge_subdomain < nEdges_owned)
4560  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = nNodes_owned + edge_subdomain;
4561  else
4562  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = ghostEdgeOffset + edge_subdomain - nEdges_owned;
4563  //unique subdomain id --> unique cross processor id
4564  //subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]] = mesh.nNodes_global + edge_global;
4565  //mwf debug
4566  // if (rank == 0)
4567  // {
4568  // std::cout<<"build loc2glob c0p2 3d eN= "<<eN<<" edge("<<nN<<","<<nN_neig<<") sub_dof= "<< subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]
4569  // <<" glob_dof= "<<subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]]<<std::endl;
4570  // }
4571  for (int eI=0; eI < 3; eI++)
4572  lagrangeNodesArray[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+local_offset+nN]*3+eI] = 0.5*(mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nN_global_subdomain*3+eI]+
4573  mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nN_neig_global_subdomain*3+eI]);
4574  }
4575 
4576  }//eN
4577 
4578  ISRestoreIndices(quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old,&quadraticNumbering_global_new2old);
4579  ISDestroy(&quadraticNumberingIS_new2old);
4580  ISDestroy(&quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old);
4581 
4582  return 0;
4583 }
4584 
4585 int buildQuadraticCubeSubdomain2GlobalMappings_3d(const MPI_Comm& PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD, Mesh& mesh,
4586  const int *edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned,
4587  const int *nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned,
4588  const int *edgeNumbering_subdomain2global,
4589  const int *nodeNumbering_subdomain2global,
4590  int& nDOF_all_processes,//total number of dofs in whole domain
4591  int& nDOF_subdomain,//total number of dofs in sub-domain
4592  int& max_dof_neighbors,//maximum number of neighbors for connectivity of dofs
4593  int *offsets_subdomain_owned, //starting point of local dofs on each processor (nProcs+1)
4594  int *subdomain_l2g, //local to global dof mapping on subdomain
4595  int *subdomain2global,//subdomain dof to global (parallel) numbering
4596  double * lagrangeNodesArray)//location of nodes corresponding to dofs
4597 {
4598  using namespace std;
4599  int ierr,size,rank;
4600 
4601  ierr = MPI_Comm_size(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,&size);
4602  ierr = MPI_Comm_rank(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,&rank);
4603 
4604  //In 2d the quadratic dofs can be associated with nodes and element Boundaries
4605  //assuming have ownership info and consistent local/global mappings for nodes, elementBoundaries
4606  //build a mapping from local quadratic dofs to global quadratic dofs for petsc
4607  //assume a processor owns a dof if it owns that node or element
4608  assert(edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned);
4609  assert(nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned);
4610  assert(edgeNumbering_subdomain2global);
4611  assert(nodeNumbering_subdomain2global);
4612  assert(mesh.subdomainp);
4613 
4614  const int *elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned=mesh.elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned;
4615  const int *elementOffsets_subdomain_owned=mesh.elementOffsets_subdomain_owned;
4616  const int *elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global=mesh.elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global;
4617  const int *elementNumbering_subdomain2global=mesh.elementNumbering_subdomain2global;
4618 
4619  const int nNodes_owned = nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank+1]-nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank];
4620  const int nEdges_owned = edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank+1]-edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank];
4621  const int nBoundaries_owned = elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank+1]-elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank];
4622  const int nElements_owned = elementOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank+1]-elementOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank];
4623 
4624  const int nDOFs_owned = nNodes_owned + nEdges_owned + nBoundaries_owned + nElements_owned;
4625  const int nDOFs_global= mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nEdges_global + mesh.nElementBoundaries_global + mesh.nElements_global;
4626  //start with a logical global ordering of dofs as
4627  //[global nodes, global edges]
4628  //want to create global numbering
4629  //[nodes proc 0,edges proc 0,nodes proc 1, edges proc 1,...]
4630  valarray<int> quadraticNumbering_new2old(nDOFs_owned);
4631  for (int nN = 0; nN < nNodes_owned; nN++)
4632  {
4633  int dof_global = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4634  quadraticNumbering_new2old[nN] = dof_global;
4635  }
4636  for (int i = 0; i < nEdges_owned; i++)
4637  {
4638  int dof_global = mesh.nNodes_global + edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4639  quadraticNumbering_new2old[nNodes_owned + i] = dof_global;
4640  }
4641 
4642  //-------------------
4643  for (int i = 0; i < nBoundaries_owned; i++)
4644  {
4645  int dof_global = mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nEdges_global + elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4646  quadraticNumbering_new2old[nNodes_owned + nEdges_owned + i] = dof_global;
4647  }
4648  for (int i = 0; i < nElements_owned; i++)
4649  {
4650  int dof_global = mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nEdges_global + mesh.nElementBoundaries_global + elementNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4651  quadraticNumbering_new2old[nNodes_owned + nEdges_owned + nBoundaries_owned + i] = dof_global;
4652  }
4653  //-------------------
4654 
4655 
4656  //build an index set for new numbering
4657  IS quadraticNumberingIS_new2old;
4658  ISCreateGeneral(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,nDOFs_owned,&quadraticNumbering_new2old[0],PETSC_COPY_VALUES,&quadraticNumberingIS_new2old);
4659  IS quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old;
4660  ISAllGather(quadraticNumberingIS_new2old,&quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old);
4661  //get old 2 new mapping for dofs
4662  const PetscInt *quadraticNumbering_global_new2old;
4663  valarray<int> quadraticNumbering_old2new_global(nDOFs_global);
4664  ISGetIndices(quadraticNumberingIS_global_new2old,&quadraticNumbering_global_new2old);
4665  for (int id = 0; id < nDOFs_global; id++)
4666  quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]] = id;
4667  //mwf debug
4668  // if (rank == 0)
4669  // {
4670  // for (int id = 0; id < nDOFs_global; id++)
4671  // {
4672  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" build 2d c0p2 mappings new2old["<<id<<"]= "<<quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]
4673  // <<" old2new["<<quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]<<"]= "<<quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[quadraticNumbering_global_new2old[id]]
4674  // <<std::endl;
4675  // }
4676  // }
4677  assert(offsets_subdomain_owned);
4678  assert(subdomain2global);
4679  assert(subdomain_l2g);
4680  assert(lagrangeNodesArray);
4681  for (int sdN=0; sdN < size+1; sdN++)
4682  offsets_subdomain_owned[sdN] = nodeOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN]+edgeOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN]+elementBoundaryOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN]+elementOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN];
4683  nDOF_all_processes = mesh.nNodes_global+mesh.nEdges_global+ mesh.nElementBoundaries_global+mesh.nElements_global;
4684  nDOF_subdomain = mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global+mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global+mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_global+mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global;
4685  max_dof_neighbors = 2*mesh.max_nNodeNeighbors_node;//8*27?
4686 
4687  //loop through owned and ghost dofs build subdomain mapping by
4688  //going from old --> new
4689  int localOffset = 0;
4690  for (int nN = 0; nN < nNodes_owned; nN++)
4691  {
4692  int dof_global_old = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4693  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4694  subdomain2global[localOffset + nN] = dof_global_new;
4695  //mwf debug
4696  // if (rank == 0)
4697  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" nN= "<<nN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+nN<<" nNodes_owned= "<<nNodes_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4698  }
4699 
4700  localOffset += nNodes_owned;
4701  for (int i = 0; i < nEdges_owned; i++)
4702  {
4703  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4704  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4705  subdomain2global[localOffset + i] = dof_global_new;
4706  //mwf debug
4707  // if (rank == 0)
4708  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" i= "<<i<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+i<<" nEdges_owned= "<<nEdges_owned
4709  // <<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4710  }
4711 
4712 
4713  localOffset += nEdges_owned;
4714  for (int i = 0; i < nBoundaries_owned; i++)
4715  {
4716  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nEdges_global + elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4717  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4718  subdomain2global[localOffset + i] = dof_global_new;
4719  //mwf debug
4720  // if (rank == 0)
4721  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" i= "<<i<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+i<<" nEdges_owned= "<<nEdges_owned
4722  // <<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4723  }
4724 
4725  localOffset += nBoundaries_owned;
4726  for (int i = 0; i < nElements_owned; i++)
4727  {
4728  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nEdges_global + mesh.nElementBoundaries_global + elementNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4729  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4730  subdomain2global[localOffset + i] = dof_global_new;
4731  //mwf debug
4732  // if (rank == 0)
4733  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" i= "<<i<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+i<<" nEdges_owned= "<<nEdges_owned
4734  // <<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4735  }
4736 
4737  localOffset += nElements_owned;
4738  for (int nN = nNodes_owned; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global; nN++)
4739  {
4740  int dof_global_old = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN];
4741  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4742  subdomain2global[localOffset + nN - nNodes_owned] = dof_global_new;
4743  //mwf debug
4744  // if (rank == 0)
4745  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" nN= "<<nN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+nN-nNodes_owned<<" nNodes_owned= "<<nNodes_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4746  }
4747 
4748  localOffset += mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global - nNodes_owned;
4749  for (int i = nEdges_owned; i < mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global; i++)
4750  {
4751  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4752  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4753  subdomain2global[localOffset + i - nEdges_owned] = dof_global_new;
4754  // //mwf debug
4755  // if (rank == 0)
4756  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" i= "<<i<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+i-nEdges_owned<<" nEdges_owned= "<<nEdges_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4757  }
4758 
4759  localOffset += mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global - nEdges_owned;
4760  for (int i = nBoundaries_owned; i < mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_global; i++)
4761  {
4762  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nEdges_global + elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4763  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4764  subdomain2global[localOffset + i - nBoundaries_owned] = dof_global_new;
4765  // //mwf debug
4766  // if (rank == 0)
4767  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" i= "<<i<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+i-nEdges_owned<<" nEdges_owned= "<<nEdges_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4768  }
4769 
4770  localOffset += mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_global - nBoundaries_owned;
4771  for (int i = nElements_owned; i < mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global; i++)
4772  {
4773  int dof_global_old = mesh.nNodes_global + mesh.nEdges_global + mesh.nElementBoundaries_global + elementNumbering_subdomain2global[i];
4774  int dof_global_new = quadraticNumbering_old2new_global[dof_global_old];
4775  subdomain2global[localOffset + i - nElements_owned] = dof_global_new;
4776  // //mwf debug
4777  // if (rank == 0)
4778  // std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" i= "<<i<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+i-nEdges_owned<<" nEdges_owned= "<<nEdges_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
4779  }
4780 
4781  //setup local to global mapping on the subdomain for finite elements
4782  const int nDOF_element = 27;
4783  const int ghostNodeOffset = nNodes_owned + nEdges_owned + nBoundaries_owned + nElements_owned;
4784  const int ghostEdgeOffset = ghostNodeOffset + mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_global-nNodes_owned;
4785  const int ghostBoundaryOffset = ghostEdgeOffset + mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global-nEdges_owned;
4786  const int ghostElementOffset = ghostBoundaryOffset + mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_global-nBoundaries_owned;
4787 
4788  int ledge[12][2] = {{0,1},{1,2},{2,3},{3,0},
4789  {0,4},{1,5},{2,6},{3,7},
4790  {4,5},{5,6},{6,7},{7,4}};
4791 
4792  int nEdges_element = 12;
4793 
4794  int lface[6][4] = {{0,1,2,3},
4795  {0,1,5,4},
4796  {1,2,6,5},
4797  {2,3,7,6},
4798  {3,0,4,7},
4799  {4,5,6,7}};
4800 
4801  assert(mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_element == 6);
4802  //need mapping from nodes to edge to setup element based relationship
4803  map<NodeTuple<2>, int> nodesEdgeMap_subdomain;
4804  for (int i=0; i < mesh.subdomainp->nEdges_global; i++)
4805  {
4806  register int nodes[2];
4807  nodes[0] = mesh.subdomainp->edgeNodesArray[2*i+0];
4808  nodes[1] = mesh.subdomainp->edgeNodesArray[2*i+1];
4809  NodeTuple<2> nt(nodes);
4810  nodesEdgeMap_subdomain[nt] = i;
4811  }
4812 
4813  map<NodeTuple<4>, int> nodesBoundaryMap_subdomain;
4814  for (int i=0; i < mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_global; i++)
4815  {
4816 
4817  register int nodes[4];
4818  nodes[0] = mesh.subdomainp->elementBoundaryNodesArray[i*4+0];
4819  nodes[1] = mesh.subdomainp->elementBoundaryNodesArray[i*4+1];
4820  nodes[2] = mesh.subdomainp->elementBoundaryNodesArray[i*4+2];
4821  nodes[3] = mesh.subdomainp->elementBoundaryNodesArray[i*4+3];
4822  NodeTuple<4> ebt(nodes);
4823  assert(nodesBoundaryMap_subdomain.find(ebt) == nodesBoundaryMap_subdomain.end());
4824  nodesBoundaryMap_subdomain[ebt] = i;
4825  }
4826 
4827  for (int eN=0; eN < mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global; eN++)
4828  {
4829  int local_offset = 0;
4830  for (int nN=0; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element; nN++)
4831  {
4832  //node_i --> unique subdomain node 0 <= i <= 3
4833  const int nN_global_subdomain = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + nN];
4834  //assign unique subdomain id based on |owned nodes|owned edges|ghost nodes|ghost edges|
4835  if (nN_global_subdomain < nNodes_owned)
4836  {
4837  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = nN_global_subdomain;
4838  }
4839  else
4840  {
4841  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = ghostNodeOffset + nN_global_subdomain - nNodes_owned;
4842  }
4843  //unique subdomain id --> unique cross processor id
4844  //subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]] = nodeNumbering_subdomain2global[nN_global_subdomain];
4845  //mwf debug
4846  // if (rank == 0)
4847  // {
4848  // std::cout<<"build loc2glob c0p2 3d eN= "<<eN<<" node= "<<nN<<" sub_dof= "<< subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]
4849  // <<" glob_dof= "<<subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]]<<std::endl;
4850  // }
4851  for (int eI=0; eI < 3; eI++)
4852  lagrangeNodesArray[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset +nN]*3+eI] = mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nN_global_subdomain*3+eI];
4853  }
4854  local_offset += mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element;
4855  for (int nN = 0; nN < nEdges_element; nN++)
4856  {
4857  register int nodes[2];
4858  nodes[0] = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + ledge[nN][0]];
4859  nodes[1] = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element + ledge[nN][1]];
4860  NodeTuple<2> nt(nodes);
4861  int edge_subdomain = nodesEdgeMap_subdomain[nt];
4862  int edge_global = edgeNumbering_subdomain2global[edge_subdomain];
4863  assert(edge_subdomain >= 0 && edge_global >= 0);
4864  //assign unique subdomain id based on |owned nodes|owned edges|ghost nodes|ghost edges|
4865  if (edge_subdomain < nEdges_owned)
4866  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = nNodes_owned + edge_subdomain;
4867  else
4868  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = ghostEdgeOffset + edge_subdomain - nEdges_owned;
4869  //unique subdomain id --> unique cross processor id
4870  //set above could do here subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]] = mesh.nNodes_global + edge_global;
4871  //mwf debug
4872  // if (rank == 0)
4873  // {
4874  // std::cout<<"build loc2glob c0p2 3d eN= "<<eN<<" edge("<<nN<<","<<nN_neig<<") sub_dof= "<< subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]
4875  // <<" glob_dof= "<<subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]]<<std::endl;
4876  // }
4877  for (int eI=0; eI < 3; eI++)
4878  lagrangeNodesArray[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+local_offset+nN]*3+eI] = 0.5*(mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nodes[0]*3+eI]+
4879  mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nodes[1]*3+eI]);
4880  }
4881 
4882  local_offset += nEdges_element;
4883  for (int nN = 0; nN < mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_element; nN++)
4884  {
4885 
4886  register int nodes[4];
4887  nodes[0] = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element+lface[nN][0]];
4888  nodes[1] = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element+lface[nN][1]];
4889  nodes[2] = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element+lface[nN][2]];
4890  nodes[3] = mesh.subdomainp->elementNodesArray[eN*mesh.subdomainp->nNodes_element+lface[nN][3]];
4891  NodeTuple<4> ebt(nodes);
4892 
4893 
4894  int boundary_subdomain = nodesBoundaryMap_subdomain[ebt];
4895  int boundary_global = elementBoundaryNumbering_subdomain2global[boundary_subdomain];
4896 
4897  assert(boundary_subdomain >= 0 && boundary_global >= 0);
4898 
4899  //assign unique subdomain id based on |owned nodes|owned edges|ghost nodes|ghost edges|
4900  if (boundary_subdomain < nBoundaries_owned)
4901  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = nNodes_owned + nEdges_owned + boundary_subdomain;
4902  else
4903  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN] = ghostBoundaryOffset + boundary_subdomain - nBoundaries_owned;
4904  //unique subdomain id --> unique cross processor id
4905  //set above could do here subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]] = mesh.nNodes_global + edge_global;
4906  //mwf debug
4907  // if (rank == 0)
4908  // {
4909  // std::cout<<"build loc2glob c0p2 3d eN= "<<eN<<" edge("<<nN<<","<<nN_neig<<") sub_dof= "<< subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]
4910  // <<" glob_dof= "<<subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]]<<std::endl;
4911  // }
4912  for (int eI=0; eI < 3; eI++)
4913  lagrangeNodesArray[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+local_offset+nN]*3+eI] = 0.25*(mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nodes[0]*3+eI]+
4914  mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nodes[1]*3+eI]+
4915  mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nodes[2]*3+eI]+
4916  mesh.subdomainp->nodeArray[nodes[3]*3+eI]);
4917  }
4918 
4919  local_offset += mesh.subdomainp->nElementBoundaries_element;
4920 
4921  // Interior node!!!
4922 
4923  if (eN < nElements_owned)
4924  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset] = nNodes_owned + nEdges_owned + nBoundaries_owned + eN;
4925  else
4926  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset] = ghostElementOffset + eN - nElements_owned;
4927  //unique subdomain id --> unique cross processor id
4928  //set above could do here subdomain2global[subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element + local_offset + nN]] = mesh.nNodes_global + edge_global;
4929  //mwf debug
4930  // if (rank == 0)
4931  // {

4959 int buildDiscontinuousGalerkinSubdomain2GlobalMappings(const MPI_Comm& PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD, Mesh& mesh,
4960  const int *elementOffsets_subdomain_owned,
4961  const int *elementNumbering_subdomain2global,
4962  int nDOF_element,
4963  int& nDOF_all_processes,//total number of dofs in whole domain
4964  int& nDOF_subdomain,//total number of dofs in sub-domain
4965  int& max_dof_neighbors,//maximum number of neighbors for connectivity of dofs
4966  int *offsets_subdomain_owned, //starting point of local dofs on each processor (nProcs+1)
4967  int * subdomain_l2g, //local to global dof mapping on subdomain
4968  int* subdomain2global)//subdomain dof to global (parallel) numbering
4969 
4970 {
4971  using namespace std;
4972  int ierr,size,rank;
4973  ierr = MPI_Comm_size(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,&size);
4974  ierr = MPI_Comm_rank(PROTEUS_COMM_WORLD,&rank);
4975 
4976  //DG dofs stored element wise
4977  //[...,eN_0,eN_1,..,eN_ndof_local,...]
4978  //assume a processor owns a dof if it owns that element
4979  assert(elementOffsets_subdomain_owned);
4980  assert(elementNumbering_subdomain2global);
4981  assert(mesh.subdomainp);
4982 
4983  const int nElements_owned = elementOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank+1]-elementOffsets_subdomain_owned[rank];
4984 
4985  assert(offsets_subdomain_owned);
4986  assert(subdomain2global);
4987  assert(subdomain_l2g);
4988  nDOF_all_processes = mesh.nElements_global*nDOF_element;
4989  nDOF_subdomain = mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global*nDOF_element;
4990  max_dof_neighbors = mesh.nElementBoundaries_element*nDOF_element;
4991 
4992  for (int sdN=0; sdN < size+1; sdN++)
4993  offsets_subdomain_owned[sdN] = elementOffsets_subdomain_owned[sdN]*nDOF_element;
4994 
4995  //loop through owned and ghost dofs build subdomain mapping
4996  for (int eN = 0; eN < mesh.subdomainp->nElements_global; eN++)
4997  {
4998  for (int i = 0; i < nDOF_element; i++)
4999  {
5000  subdomain2global[eN*nDOF_element + i] = elementNumbering_subdomain2global[eN]*nDOF_element + i;
5001  //mwf debug
5002  //std::cout<<" rank= "<<rank<<" eN= "<<eN<<" local dof= "<<localOffset+eN<<" nElements_owned= "<<nElements_owned<<" dof_old= "<<dof_global_old<<" new= "<<dof_global_new<<std::endl;
5003  subdomain_l2g[eN*nDOF_element+i] = eN*nDOF_element + i;
5004  }
5005  }
5006 
5007  return 0;
5008 }
